      //Ready callback for Kaltura player
      function jsCallbackReady() {
          try {
            var eventMap = {
                "trailerTakeoverKaltura": {
                    "playerPlayEnd": "trailerTakeoverComplete"
                },
                "videoPlayerSwf": {
                    "playerPlayEnd": "changeMedia"
                },
                "trackPlayerKaltura": {
                    "playerPlayEnd": "trackPlayerComplete"
                }
            };
            
            var el;
            for (id in eventMap) {
                el = document.getElementById(id);
                if (el && el.addJsListener) {
                    for (event in eventMap[id]) {
                        el.addJsListener(event, eventMap[id][event])
                    }
                }
            }
          } catch(e) {}
      }

      <div class="noprint"> 
       <div>
        <b>Scope of Privacy Policy</b>
       </div> Your privacy is important to us. This notice provides highlights of Warner Bros. Entertainment Inc.'s (&quot;WBEI&quot;, &quot;we,&quot; &quot;our,&quot; &quot;us&quot;) 
       <a href="#p0">Privacy Policy</a>. Our full Privacy Policy applies to WBEI Web sites (&quot;Site&quot; or &quot;Sites&quot;) and services that display or link to this policy. To review our children's privacy practices, please view our 
       <a href="#children">Additional information regarding children.</a> 
       <br /> 
       <a href="#p0">WBEI's Full Privacy Policy</a> 
       <div class="privacyheader">
        PRIVACY POLICY HIGHLIGHTS
       </div> 
       <div class="leftcol"> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          INFORMATION COLLECTION
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <ul> 
           <li>When you register or engage with our Sites, such as by participating in contests, sweepstakes or promotions, we may ask you to provide personally identifiable information (e.g., name, address, e-mail, phone number, location data, credit card information, and information about your interests in our products and services) to access certain content, features, and functionality.</li> 
           <li>We may collect additional information from you if you access our Sites through a mobile device (e.g. unique device identifier, device’s operating system, mobile carrier).</li> 
           <li>You may also provide us with information when interacting with our content through or linking to third-party social media sites, plug-ins, or applications.</li> 
           <li>The information we collect may be combined with information from outside records. <br /><a href="#p1">More Info</a></li> 
           <li>We use cookies and other similar technologies to keep track of your interactions with our Sites and to offer you a more personalized experience. <br /><a href="#cookies">More Info</a></li> 
          </ul> 
          <br /> 
          <span><a href="#p1">Additional Information</a></span> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          USES OF INFORMATION
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <ul> 
           <li>The information we collect is used to fulfill your requests, to develop, protect, maintain, improve, and provide our products, programs, and services, and to operate our business. This includes displaying personalized content and advertising to provide you with the messages we think you will find most interesting.</li> 
           <li>We and our affiliates and business partners may also use this information to inform you of other products or services that may interest you.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <br /> 
          <span><a href="#infouse">Additional Information</a></span> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          IMPORTANT ADDITIONAL INFORMATION
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <ul> 
           <li>Our full WBEI Privacy Policy contains links to additional information about specific Sites and privacy practices.</li> 
           <li>We take reasonable measures designed to safeguard the information we collect online through our Sites. <br /><a href="#security">More Info</a></li> 
           <li>WBEI operates globally, so the information we collect may be sent to our servers in the U.S. See the International Transfers section of our policy. <br /><a href="#international">More Info</a></li> 
          </ul> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="rightcol"> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          YOUR CHOICES
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <ul> 
           <li>If you decide you no longer want to receive our promotional e-mails, simply follow the instructions in that e-mail.</li> 
           <li>To make choices about how we share information with third parties, such as our business partners, simply log into your account if you have created one with us or e-mail us at <a href="mailto:privacy@wb.com">privacy@wb.com</a><br /><a href="#yourchoices">More Info</a></li> 
           <li>To review and edit personally identifiable information you have provided, go to the <a href="#infoaccess">How to Access or Correct Your Information</a> of our full Privacy Policy.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <br /> 
          <span><a href="#yourchoices">Additional Information</a></span> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          DISCLOSURE OF INFORMATION
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <span>We may share personally identifiable information:</span>
          <br />
          <br /> 
          <ul> 
           <li>Where we have your consent (e.g., opt-in, opt-out, preferences).</li> 
           <li>With third-party service providers and other companies that work on our behalf or with our affiliates.</li> 
           <li>With business partners, such as those who sponsor a sweepstakes, contest or promotion or those who jointly offer an activity or service.</li> 
           <li>In the event of a corporate transaction (e.g., merger or sale).</li> 
           <li>When required by law or public authorities.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <br /> 
          <span><a href="#infosharing">Additional Information</a></span> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="highlightbox"> 
         <div class="highlighttitle">
          HOW TO CONTACT US
         </div> 
         <div class="highlightcontent"> 
          <span>For more information about our privacy practices, go to our full WBEI Privacy Policy, write us using our <a href="/help/customer-service.html">Web form</a> or send an email to <a href="mailto:privacy@wb.com">privacy@wb.com</a></span>

        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>Registration and account information. </b>At some Sites, you can order products, play games, read critic and user reviews, enter contests, vote in polls, rate movies, TV shows and other content, or otherwise express an opinion, subscribe to one of our services such as our online newsletters, or participate in one of our online forums or communities. In the course of using our Sites, we may ask you to create an account or register for an application by providing us with certain personally identifiable information that can be used to contact or identify you, as well as to administer your account. The types of personally identifiable information that you provide as part of your account may include: name, address, e-mail address, telephone number, fax number, credit card and billing information, information about your interest in and use of various content, products, programs, and services, and other information that you provide to us.</font></p>

The types of personally identifiable information that may be collected about other people as part of this process include recipient's name, address, e-mail address, telephone number, and information about the recipient’s interest in and use of various content, products, programs, and services. </font></p>

You may also choose to link your account with us to third party social media sites. When you link your account or engage with our content on or through third party social media sites, services, plug-ins, or applications you may allow us to have ongoing access to certain information from your social media account (e.g., name, e-mail address, profile photo, gender, birthday, location, your list of friends and their contact information, people you follow and/or who follow you, the posts or the 'likes' you make).         <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>COOKIES AND OTHER TECHNICAL INFORMATION</b> </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>Cookies and Web beacons.</b> We, and our affiliates, third party service providers, and our business partners may send &quot;cookies&quot; to your computer or use similar technologies to enhance your online experience at our Sites. &quot;Cookies&quot; are files that can identify you as a unique customer and store your personal preferences as well as technical information (including click through and click stream data). Cookies manage and measure the performance of advertisements displayed on or delivered by or through us and/or other networks or sites. Cookies can either be persistent (i.e., they remain on your computer until you delete them) or temporary (i.e., they last only until you close your browser).</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">Some of our Sites may use locally stored objects (sometimes referred to as &quot;Flash cookies&quot;) to provide certain content, such as video on demand, video clips, or animation. Adobe's Flash player and similar applications use this technology to remember settings, preferences, and usage similar to browser cookies. Flash cookies are not managed through your web browser, but you can access your Flash management tools from <a href="http://www.macromedia.com/support/documentation/en/flashplayer/help/settings_manager07.html" target="_blank">Adobe's web site</a>.</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">We may also use &quot;Web beacons&quot; that monitor your use of our Sites. Web beacons (or Web bugs) are small strings of code that provide a method for delivering a graphic image on a Web page for the purpose of transferring data, such as the IP (Internet Protocol) address of the computer that downloaded the page on which the Web beacon appears, the URL (Uniform Resource Locator) of the page on which the Web beacon appears, the time the page containing the Web beacon was viewed, the types of browser that fetched the Web beacon and the identification number of any cookie on the computer previously placed by that server. </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">When corresponding with you via HTML capable email, Web beacons let us know whether you received and opened our email.</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">On their own, cookies or Web beacons do not contain or reveal any personally identifiable information. However, if you choose to furnish personally identifiable information, this information can be linked to the data stored in the cookies/Web beacons.</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>Managing cookies and Web beacons </b><font kerning="0"><b>and Do Not Track</b></font><b>. </b>By accepting this Privacy Policy, you specifically agree to our use of cookies and Web beacons as described herein. You may adjust your browser to reject cookies from us or from any other Web site. Additionally, by setting your Web browser to display HTML emails as text only, you may be able to prevent the use of some Web beacons. Please consult the &quot;Help&quot; section of your browser for more information. However, certain areas of our Sites can only be accessed in conjunction with cookies or similar devices and you should be aware that disabling cookies or similar devices might prevent you from accessing some of our content or Site features. <font kerning="0">We do not currently take actions to respond to Do Not Track signals because a uniform technological standard has not yet been developed. We continue to review new technologies and may adopt a standard once one is created.<font kerning="1"></font></font></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"> <a name="security"></a></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>OUR COMMITMENT TO SECURITY</b> &nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">We have put in place reasonable physical, electronic, and managerial procedures designed to safeguard the information we collect online at the Sites. However, we cannot assure you that personally identifiable information that we collect will never be used or disclosed in a manner that is inconsistent with this Privacy Policy.</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><a name="infoaccess"></a></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>HOW YOU CAN ACCESS OR CORRECT INFORMATION</b> &nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">To access the personally identifiable information that our Sites have collected about you online from the pages on which this Privacy Policy is posted, to correct factual errors in such information, or to update your interests, preferences or other portions of your user profile, please log into your account if you have created one with us or send an email to <a href="mailto:privacy@wb.com" target="_blank">privacy@wb.com</a>.</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">To help protect your privacy and security, we will take reasonable steps to help verify your identity before granting access or making corrections. </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"> <a name="children"></a></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp; </font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">&nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"></font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1"><b>ADDITIONAL INFORMATION REGARDING CHILDREN'S PRIVACY</b> &nbsp;</font></p>
       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">Visitors to this Site may participate in many activities without providing any personally identifiable information. However, in some cases if a user wants to participate in certain of our interactive features, we ask the user to register and provide us with the following information: the user's email address and age information. When the person who registers indicates that he or she is under 13 years old, we will either (i) collect no or limited personally identifiable information (e.g. e-mail address only) from that individual, (ii) inform the child that a parent's verifiable consent is required, or (iii) collect the email address of the user's parent in addition to the user's email address. We use the parent's email address to seek the parent's verifiable consent or notify the parent of his/her child's online activities and enable the parent to unsubscribe his/her child from a newsletter or other similar activity. If a user is under 13, we will not condition his/her participation in an online activity on the disclosure of more information than is reasonably necessary to participate in the activity. We do not share children's information with outside third parties not bound by this Privacy Policy for their own marketing purposes. If you would like to review any personally identifiable information that we have collected online from your child, have this information deleted from our active servers, and/or request that there be no further collection or use of your child's information or if you have questions about these information practices, you may contact us at <a href="mailto:privacy@wb.com" target="_blank">privacy@wb.com</a>, or at Warner Bros. Advanced Digital Services, a division of Warner Bros. Technical Operations Inc., Attention. Chief Privacy Officer, 4000 Warner Blvd., Bldg. 168, Burbank, CA 91522, (818) 977-0018. </font></p>

       </textformat>
       <textformat leading="2">
        <p align="LEFT"><font face="Arial" size="10" color="#000000" letterspacing="0" kerning="1">As we operate internationally, and many of our computer systems are currently based in the United States, your personally identifiable information will be processed by us in the U.S. where data protection and privacy regulations may not offer the same level of protection as in other parts of the world, such as the European Union. If you create a user account with our Sites as a visitor from outside the United States, you consent to the collection and/or processing in the United States of your personally identifiable information, which includes the use of cookies as described above. ?</font></p>

     <img src="/Images/Scheduling.jpg" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>We Give Your Course a Home</h3> 
      <br /> 
      <h4>Academic Scheduling serves you by:</h4> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>Scheduling academic course activities (lectures, discussions) in general assignment classrooms for winter, spring and fall quarters.</li> 
       <li>Scheduling one-time events tied to academic courses (review sessions, guest speakers) for winter, spring and fall quarters.</li> 
       <li>Providing training for the course-scheduling component of the Student Information System (SIS).</li> 
       <li>Connecting you to classroom technology and maintenance support.</li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <img src="/Images/paperpushpin.png" style="float: right; margin: 4px;" /> 
       <div class="title">
         Helpful Resources: 
       </div> 
       <ul class="helpfulResourcesImage"> 
        <li><a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://hub.ucr.edu/EventScheduling/Pages/CommonsEventScheduling.aspx">Highlander Event Scheduling</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://cnc.ucr.edu/multimedia/">Multimedia Technologies</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://rspace.ucr.edu">R'Space</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/crams/default.aspx">CRAMS</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-17 last"> 
      <h4>Explore Available Classrooms</h4> 
      <p>We have 87 general assignment classrooms, ranging in size from 10 to 570 seats. Explore available classrooms, seating capacities, room layouts and media options with <a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms.</a></p> 
      <h4>Schedule Academic Course Activities</h4> 
      <p>If you have been designated to schedule your department’s course activities, we can help connect you to training and explain how the process works. <a href="scheduling-academic-course-activities.aspx">Learn more.</a></p> 
      <h4>One-Time Events, Media and Maintenance</h4> 
      <p>Request rooms for <a href="one-time-events.aspx">one-time events</a> and get <a href="media-and-maintenance.aspx">technology and maintenance support</a> for your classroom.</p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p>

       <p class="footer_info"> <img src="/Images/saBldImage_registrar.jpg" width="120" height="87" alt="Student Serves Building" />The Office of the Registrar delivers accurate, prompt, courteous and consistent services to all students and constituents of UC Riverside. The Registrar takes a leadership role in management of registration, student academic records, course and classroom scheduling, classroom utilization, publications production, and data distribution. </p>

    <div id="main"> 
     <p> <img src="/resources/images/home_main.jpg" alt="." width="484" height="180" /> </p> 
     <h3>What Makes UCR So Great?</h3> 
     <p> It's not just the world-class faculty and facilities that make UC Riverside the place to be — it's also the thriving arts community, the one-of-a-kind special collections and lecture series that attract experts from around the world. It's the concerts, film festivals, dazzling dance performances and thought-provoking theater. It's the beauty of our Botanic Gardens and famed 22-acre Citrus Variety Collection. It's the Campus Store and KUCR, our own non-commercial radio station playing cutting-edge music. And, of course, it's the UCR Libraries, with over two million volumes and home to the world's largest cataloged collection of science fiction and fantasy. </p> 
     <h4>And we're just getting started!</h4> 
     <h3 class="section">Discover what UCR has to Offer!</h3> 
     <ul class="inline"> 
      <li><a class="img_link" title="Libraries" href="/resources/libraries/"><img src="/resources/images/bttn_box_libraries.gif" alt="Libraries" width="158" height="105" /></a></li> 
      <li><a class="img_link" title="ARTSblock" href="/resources/art_culture/artsblock.html"><img class="img_link" src="/resources/images/bttn_box_artsblock.gif" alt="ARTSblock" width="169" height="105" /></a></li> 
      <li><a class="img_link" title="Botanic Gardens" href="/resources/botanic_gardens.html"><img class="img_link" src="/resources/images/bttn_box_botanic.gif" alt="Botanic Gardens" width="157" height="105" /></a></li> 
      <li><a class="img_link" title="Campus Store" href="/resources/campus_store.html"><img src="/resources/images/bttn_box_store.gif" alt="Campus Store" width="158" height="105" /></a></li>

     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/macy.css" cssmenu="" width="790" --> 
     <div class="header"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="title" group="Everyone" button="734" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" --> 
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div -->
     </div> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="maincontent" group="Everyone" button="657" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" --> 
      <p><a href="http://amd.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Application &amp; Multimedia Development</a> provides innovative and creative full service web and graphic design for the UCR campus and community. Our knowledgeable and diverse staff is committed to promoting UCR's digital future. With fully integrated, back-end programming solutions tailored to each client's specific needs, we push the university's academic outreach efforts beyond the top level of even the private sector. Our services are available to faculty, staff, departments, organizations and groups on campus.</p> 
      <h3>Mission Statement</h3> 
      <p>AMD will achieve the best possible web presence for our clients with attractive, dynamic designs and captivating, intuitive websites. With our client's needs in mind, we strive to create messages that are clear, concise, unique, and effective.</p> 
      <h3>Services</h3> 
      <ul class="big_links"> 
       <li><a href="/amd/amd_3d.html"><img src="/images/3dthumb.jpg" alt="3D animation" width="131" height="68" /><strong>3D Modeling and Animations </strong>Application and Multimedia Development can punch up your presentations, publication material, videos and animations with state-of-the-art 3D graphics. </a></li> 
       <li><a href="/amd/amd_hosting.html"><img src="/images/mousethumb.jpg" alt="Website hosting" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Faculty Website Hosting </strong>As a faculty member at UC Riverside, you get free web hosting for your research page or instructional page. You will need a UCR Net ID. </a></li> 
       <li><a href="/amd/amd_graphics.html"><img src="/images/graphicthumb.jpg" alt="Graphic design" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Graphic Design </strong>AMD offers innovative and creative graphic design services rating at the top of the private industry. Our artists have outstanding backgrounds in traditional disciplines such as drawing, painting, sculpture, and photography.</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/amd/amd_appdev.html"><img src="/images/applicationthumb.jpg" alt="Application Development" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Application Development </strong>Many departments need Internet and Intranet applications. Most departments are non-technical in nature. Due to this need and demand, AMD is now providing application development for the UCR campus.</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/amd/amd_webcontent.html"><img src="/images/lightthumb.jpg" alt="Creative Ideas" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Web Content Creation</strong> In addition to web hosting and development services, C&amp;C can work with you to develop compelling content for your site and keep it up-to-date. </a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Staff</h3> 
      <div class="spotlight"> 
       <h3>Application &amp; Multimedia Development</h3> 
       <p><a href="http://www.campusmap.ucr.edu/campusMap.php?loc=CCCTR" target="_blank">Computing &amp; Communications Building</a><br /> Office Hours: M-F 9:00a-6:00p<br /> Fax: (951) 827-4541</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="contact-us"> 
       <h3>Management</h3> 
       <p>Eric Martin, Manager<br /> Email: <a href="mailto:eric@ucr.edu">eric.martin@ucr.edu</a></p> 
       <h3>Programming</h3> 
       <p>Juan Gonzales, Lead Developer<br /> Email: <a href="mailto:juan.gonzales@ucr.edu">juan.gonzalez@ucr.edu</a></p> 
       <p>Tom Hsu, Senior Application Developer<br /> Email: <a href="mailto:tom.hsu@ucr.edu">tom.hsu@ucr.edu</a></p> 
       <p>Jack Cui, Programmer<br /> Email: <a href="mailto:jack.cui@ucr.edu">jack.cui@ucr.edu</a></p> 
       <p>Sumita Roy Chowdhury, Application Developer<br /> Email: <a href="mailto:sumita.roychowdhury@ucr.edu">sumita.roychowdhury@ucr.edu</a></p> 
       <h3>Graphics</h3> 
       <p>Sohail Wasif, Senior Graphics Designer<br /> Email: <a href="http://mce_host/maitlto:sohail.wasif@ucr.edu">sohail.wasif@ucr.edu</a></p>
